## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="0c85a-796">Atributos de Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0c85a-796">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0c85a-797">Esta clase contiene los siguientes atributos para Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0c85a-797">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
